During the current Covid 19 pandemic we find ourselves in, you would think that they would be on top of their game regarding covid 19 symptoms, inaccurate test results, and up to date information surrounding the virus such as is related to Covid 19 long haulers. Before July 15th I was a straight A college student on my last year of community college in addittion to being very active, as I mountianbiked 90 miles per week!!!! I was in bed for 2 months straight and its been almost 6 months since I came down with this illness. I have been to the E.R at least if not over 15 times within these 6 months and they tell me there is nothing wrong with me every single time. At this point I have been in there so many times that Doctors and nurses belittle me and talk down on me in a condescending manner, basically telling me its all in my head despite current up-to-date information on Covid long haulers and their struggle and symptoms. < text>
My wife and I were on a family vacation in the Tahoe Donner area when suddenly she became ill. This was on Saint Patrick's Day, a Sunday.
I am a physician and suspected she might have appendicitis and was concerned about bringing her to TFH because I thought a small hospital in the mountains might not have the appropriate physicians, lab, Xray,etc.
Boy were we surprised!
Despite being extremely busy due to many orthopedic and other emergencies filling the ER, my wife was seen and evaluated within a few hours. Dr. Claire Johnson was very kind and ordered the necessary labs and a CT scan which confirmed appendicitis.
Dr. Crystine Lee was the surgeon on call who came and offered antibiotic therapy or appendectomy. Since we had driven from Florida, my wife opted for appendectomy which was performed that night. I couldn't believe we got a Stanford and UCSF trained surgeon who did a fellowship in laparoscopic surgery to do the surgery on a Sunday night, a holiday at that. With Dr. Lee's exceptional training, we felt it best to have her do the surgery rather than taking the chance of the antibiotics not working or having a flare up while we were driving back to Florida.
The anesthesiologist, Dr. Bany, did a thorough pre-op evaluation and we felt very comfortable with her doing the anesthesia.
Not knowing much about the hospital, I decided to spend the night in my wife's room just to keep an eye on things.
Turns out that was unnecessary because her night nurse, Rob, was fantastic. He was so attentive and made us feel completely safe!
From my 37 years of experience as a physician, I know that nurses are the front line of patient care in a hospital setting. A good nurse can save a patient from disaster.
My wife went home the next day and the day nurse, Brad, also seemed highly talented and made us feel at ease.
From start to finish, Tahoe Forest Hospital provided exceptional care to my wife.
Appendicitis is still a life threatening condition, especially if there is a delay in diagnosis or treatment.
We will be forever grateful to Tahoe Forest Hospital and it's excellent staff.
Brian McNulty, M.D.<//text>

< Text>
I've been hunting for good Philly cheese steak sandwiches for as long as I can remember. I've tried almost every place that serves these sandwiches from Santa Barbara to van nuys. I finally no longer have to drive to McMasters at UCSB to get a great Philly cheese steak sandwich.

This place nailed it. Soft delicious roll, perfectly sliced and grilled ribeye, veggies, and of course, the wiz. The flavors are perfectly balanced, and the sandwich is constructed very well. Good proportions of vegetables to meat and bread, juicy but not soggy.

What really sets this place apart from all the rest is the absolutely amazing staff. I called them about six minutes before they were closing on a Saturday, the person who answered was friendly, and sounded genuinely happy about the fact that I wanted to place an order for pickup. I told them I was about 10 minutes away, and asked if it was still okay to place the pickup order, and was told to not worry about it and just to come on in. That really made me feel good about ordering.

When I arrived the place was still buzzing with customers and my order was almost ready. By the time I finished paying, it was done. Do yourself a favor and come try the food at this place, you won't be disappointed.</Text>
